```

sudo systemctl status shelfeye
```

You should now see it as **active (running)** instead of the exit-code error. Once it's running, you'll be able to access the application at `http://naniwatanacheck.local:5000`.

If you want to watch it start up in real-time, you can run:

```bash
sudo journalctl -u shelfeye -f
```

This will show you the live logs as the service starts. You should see messages about checking for updates, syncing the database, and finally "serving on port 5000".
